+# Fix for ZipArchiveFuzzer Assertion Failure
+
+## Issue
+The fuzzer discovered an assertion failure in `Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.TryReadBlock`:
+```
+Assertion failed: zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null
+```
+
+## Root Cause
+The crash input contains:
+1. A malformed End of Central Directory (EOCD) with `0xFFFF` entries, indicating Zip64 format is needed
+2. A Zip64 EOCD Locator signature (`PK\x06\x07`) at offset 25
+3. **Only 12 bytes available** after the signature, but **20 bytes are required** for a complete Zip64 EOCD Locator
+
+### Code Flow (Before Fix)
+1. `SeekBackwardsToSignature()` finds the Zip64 EOCD Locator signature → returns `true`
+2. `TryReadBlock()` is called, assuming the block is valid
+3. `ReadAtLeast()` tries to read 20 bytes, but only gets 12 bytes (EOF)
+4. `TryReadBlockCore()` returns `false` because `bytesRead < TotalSize`
+5. `Debug.Assert(zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null)` **FAILS**
+6. **CRASH** with assertion failure in debug builds
+
+## The Fix
+Replace the `Debug.Assert` with proper error handling:
+
+### Before:
+```csharp
+public static Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator TryReadBlock(Stream stream)
+{
+    Span<byte> blockContents = stackalloc byte[TotalSize];
+    int bytesRead = stream.ReadAtLeast(blockContents, blockContents.Length, throwOnEndOfStream: false);
+    bool zip64eocdLocatorProper = TryReadBlockCore(blockContents, bytesRead, out Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator? zip64EOCDLocator);
+
+    Debug.Assert(zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null);
+
+    return zip64EOCDLocator;
+}
+```
+
+### After:
+```csharp
+public static Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator TryReadBlock(Stream stream)
+{
+    Span<byte> blockContents = stackalloc byte[TotalSize];
+    int bytesRead = stream.ReadAtLeast(blockContents, blockContents.Length, throwOnEndOfStream: false);
+    if (!TryReadBlockCore(blockContents, bytesRead, out Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator? zip64EOCDLocator))
+    {
+        throw new InvalidDataException(SR.Zip64EOCDNotWhereExpected);
+    }
+
+    return zip64EOCDLocator;
+}
+```
+
+## Changes Made
+1. **ZipBlocks.cs**: Modified `Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.TryReadBlock()` to throw `InvalidDataException` instead of using `Debug.Assert`
+2. **ZipBlocks.Async.cs**: Modified `Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.TryReadBlockAsync()` with the same fix
+
+## Rationale
+1. **Consistency**: The fix makes `Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.TryReadBlock` consistent with `Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryRecord.TryReadBlock`, which already throws `InvalidDataException` on malformed data
+2. **Proper Error Handling**: External data (ZIP file contents) should never cause assertion failures. Invalid data should throw exceptions that can be caught and handled
+3. **Security**: Prevents crashes from malformed ZIP files in production builds
+4. **Matches Intent**: The comment in `TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectory` says "if we don't find the Zip64-EOCD, we just give up and try to use the original values", indicating graceful handling was intended
+
+## Testing
+The fix handles these edge cases:
+- ✓ Zip64 EOCD Locator signature present but insufficient data (original crash case)
+- ✓ Just signature with no data after it
+- ✓ Partial data (< 20 bytes)
+- ✓ Valid complete locator (20 bytes) continues to work
+
+## Impact
+- **Before**: Crash with assertion failure in debug builds, undefined behavior in release builds
+- **After**: Throws `InvalidDataException` with clear error message, properly handled by calling code
+- **No breaking changes**: The exception is already expected and handled by the calling code in `TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectory`

+// Simple test to verify the crash fix
+using System;
+using System.IO;
+using System.IO.Compression;
+
+namespace TestCrashFix
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static int Main()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("Testing Zip64 EOCD Locator crash fix...");
+            
+            // The crash input from the issue (Base64: UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ==)
+            // This contains:
+            // - A malformed EOCD at offset 1 with 0xFFFF entries (indicating Zip64)
+            // - A Zip64 EOCD Locator signature at offset 25, but only 12 bytes available (needs 20)
+            byte[] crashData = new byte[] {
+                0x50, 0x50, 0x4b, 0x05, 0x06, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x58, 0x69,
+                0x04, 0x61, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x50, 0x4b, 0x06, 0x07, 0x00, 0x00, 0x4b,
+                0x05, 0x06, 0xff, 0xff, 0x05
+            };
+            
+            Console.WriteLine($"Testing with {crashData.Length} bytes of malformed ZIP data");
+            Console.WriteLine($"Data contains Zip64 EOCD Locator signature but insufficient bytes");
+            
+            bool testPassed = false;
+            
+            try
+            {
+                using (var ms = new MemoryStream(crashData))
+                {
+                    using (var zip = new ZipArchive(ms, ZipArchiveMode.Read, false))
+                    {
+                        Console.WriteLine("ERROR: Should have thrown an exception but didn't!");
+                        return 1;
+                    }
+                }
+            }
+            catch (InvalidDataException ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"✓ SUCCESS: Got expected InvalidDataException");
+                Console.WriteLine($"  Message: {ex.Message}");
+                testPassed = true;
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"✗ ERROR: Got unexpected exception type: {ex.GetType().Name}");
+                Console.WriteLine($"  Message: {ex.Message}");
+                Console.WriteLine($"  StackTrace:\n{ex.StackTrace}");
+                return 1;
+            }
+            
+            if (testPassed)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("\n✓ Test PASSED - The crash fix is working correctly!");
+                return 0;
+            }
+            else
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("\n✗ Test FAILED");
+                return 1;
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import base64
+import subprocess
+import sys
+import os
+
+# The crash input from the issue
+crash_input_base64 = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ=="
+
+# Decode and write to a file
+crash_data = base64.b64decode(crash_input_base64)
+with open('/tmp/crash_input.bin', 'wb') as f:
+    f.write(crash_data)
+
+print("Created crash input file")
+print(f"Size: {len(crash_data)} bytes")
+print(f"Hex: {crash_data.hex()}")
+
+# Create a simple C# test program
+cs_program = """
+using System;
+using System.IO;
+using System.IO.Compression;
+
+class Program
+{
+    static int Main(string[] args)
+    {
+        if (args.Length < 1)
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("Usage: program <file>");
+            return 1;
+        }
+        
+        try
+        {
+            using (var fs = File.OpenRead(args[0]))
+            {
+                using (var zip = new ZipArchive(fs, ZipArchiveMode.Read, false))
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine("Successfully opened zip archive");
+                    return 0;
+                }
+            }
+        }
+        catch (InvalidDataException ex)
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine($"Expected InvalidDataException: {ex.Message}");
+            return 0; // Expected error
+        }
+        catch (Exception ex)
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine($"Unexpected exception: {ex.GetType().Name}: {ex.Message}");
+            Console.WriteLine($"StackTrace: {ex.StackTrace}");
+            return 1;
+        }
+    }
+}
+"""
+
+# Find the test project
+testbed = "/testbed"
+test_project = os.path.join(testbed, "src/libraries/System.IO.Compression.Tests/System.IO.Compression.Tests.csproj")
+
+if os.path.exists(test_project):

+    print("\nBuilding System.IO.Compression library...")
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ['dotnet', 'build', os.path.join(testbed, 'src/libraries/System.IO.Compression/src/System.IO.Compression.csproj')],
+        capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=120
+    )
+    if result.returncode != 0:
+        print("Build failed!")
+        print(result.stdout[-500:] if len(result.stdout) > 500 else result.stdout)
+        print(result.stderr[-500:] if len(result.stderr) > 500 else result.stderr)
+        sys.exit(1)
+    print("Build succeeded!")
+
+# Create a minimal test app
+test_app_dir = '/tmp/zip_test_app'
+os.makedirs(test_app_dir, exist_ok=True)
+

+    f.write("""

+  <PropertyGroup>
+    <OutputType>Exe</OutputType>
+    <TargetFramework>net8.0</TargetFramework>
+    <AllowUnsafeBlocks>true</AllowUnsafeBlocks>
+  </PropertyGroup>
+</Project>
+""")
+
+with open(os.path.join(test_app_dir, 'Program.cs'), 'w') as f:
+    f.write(cs_program)
+
+print("\nBuilding test application...")
+result = subprocess.run(

+)
